  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_778a2058-47a4-408c-b454-affc0c0db39c'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer11444378435384627288">Roiling in political corruption and the raging violence of drug cartels in the California/Mexico borderlands, Twisted Love explores the redemptive power of love even amidst the most brutal and privileged echelons of contemporary society. Julietta Aguilar, a young archaeologist with a dark past shrouded with sordid family secrets, discovers a hidden chamber under the ruins </span>
  <span id="freeText11444378435384627288" style="display:none">Roiling in political corruption and the raging violence of drug cartels in the California/Mexico borderlands, Twisted Love explores the redemptive power of love even amidst the most brutal and privileged echelons of contemporary society. Julietta Aguilar, a young archaeologist with a dark past shrouded with sordid family secrets, discovers a hidden chamber under the ruins of the Templo Mejor, in the heart of Mexico City. She soon finds herself enmeshed in an ancient mystery even as she tries to solve her father's senseless murder.Now followed by cartel killers, deadly supernatural spirits and thwarted by her own family, her quest for peace seems almost insurmountable - until she meets a man in black with a nefarious background who goes only by one name. Rocky. A fast-paced, gripping read reminiscent of fifties pulp, the characters in Twisted Love offer a dark study in human nature, with all the gory details of unbridled power, soul-searching hatred, strange fetishes, and macabre personalities etched on the reader's mind in searing black and white.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11444378435384627288" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3178245718?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/28513574-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28513574-brenna?shelf=autographed">autographed</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28513574-brenna?shelf=print-from-author">print-from-author</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3178245718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1708944875208957100">Julietta is an archeologist. Rocky is an ex-Marine turned hired killer. Set in Mexico, the stories of these 2 characters are, initially, separated. Eventually, the stories intersect, but not without a mix of the Mexican Drug Cartel, dirty cops, bloodshed, and the possibility of bringing forth some Aztec spirits. <br/>Yes, the story has bloodshed. Yes, there are some gritty scenes in the book. Yes, there are prostitution and drug scenes in the book. The characters of Julietta and Rocky are well develo</span>
  <span id="freeText1708944875208957100" style="display:none">Julietta is an archeologist. Rocky is an ex-Marine turned hired killer. Set in Mexico, the stories of these 2 characters are, initially, separated. Eventually, the stories intersect, but not without a mix of the Mexican Drug Cartel, dirty cops, bloodshed, and the possibility of bringing forth some Aztec spirits. <br />Yes, the story has bloodshed. Yes, there are some gritty scenes in the book. Yes, there are prostitution and drug scenes in the book. The characters of Julietta and Rocky are well developed, passionate about what they do. Runnels works in a good twist or two of who is double-crossing who. Both Rocky and Julietta have a dark side, but both have heart, with a desire to get past the negativity in their world and move forward. <br /><i> <u>Twisted Love</u></i> moves quickly and will keep your attention. I kept it with me in my car and at home so whenever I did sit and read, the book was right there. <br /><br />***I received a copy of this from Wally Runnels. Thanks to M. M. Hudson, as well, for chance to read and review this book.***</span>

<div id="review_3125827446" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3125827446" />
    <a title="M.M. Hudson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15155456-m-m-hudson"><img alt="M.M. Hudson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575089849p2/15155456.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3125827446?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M.M. Hudson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M.M. Hudson" href="/user/show/15155456-m-m-hudson">M.M. Hudson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3125827446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4633709693236771662">This book is incredibly gritty. It delves into a story of love, lust, hard work, pain, and life in the underworld of drugs and killing. The title of the book somewhat makes you believe that love will prevail with a bit of a twist. It is that for sure but it does not really give hint at how twisted it is. The characters are well developed and believable. Some characters I felt pain for, others, I loathed.<br/><br/>There are scenes in the book that are hard to swallow and at times I wanted to throw up at th</span>
  <span id="freeText4633709693236771662" style="display:none">This book is incredibly gritty. It delves into a story of love, lust, hard work, pain, and life in the underworld of drugs and killing. The title of the book somewhat makes you believe that love will prevail with a bit of a twist. It is that for sure but it does not really give hint at how twisted it is. The characters are well developed and believable. Some characters I felt pain for, others, I loathed.<br /><br />There are scenes in the book that are hard to swallow and at times I wanted to throw up at the thought of them. Yet, they were written with true imaginative power and not so graphically. The author was brilliant how he wrote those scenes and the love scene that was in the book as well. I enjoyed the twists of them.<br /><br />Do not get me wrong though, this is no romance novel! The author does a great job at picturing what it might be like to live as an archaeologist and what dangers it could impose. He manages to twist ancient theories of the Aztec people with a ghostly dig. He gets political corruption in there too. If that is not enough, there is also an intertwined story of an ex-marine turned hired blood-cold killer, turned conscientious lover into the story. I was truly amazed how it all came together in the end.<br /><br />This book is one roller coaster of a ride that was really hard to put down at times. However, I had to because there is so much, that i had to breathe on occasion just to grasp it all.<br /><br />Do you want a great thriller to read? Then this is the book for you. 5 stars!<br /><br />NOTE: I do want to warn my readers of some possible triggers: Graphic murder scenes, uncomfortable sex scenes, and language.<br /><br />Disclosure: I received a copy of this book from the author. The views expressed here are 100% my own and may differ with yours. ~Michelle</span>
  <a data-text-id="4633709693236771662" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1909549347877949631">Twisted Love by Wally Runnels is a gritty tale that is enmeshed around the drug cartels in Mexico. Rocky is a force to be reckoned with and as a creepy one armed assassin and a ex- marine, he is a gifted killer.   <span id="freeText1909549347877949631" style="display:none">Twisted Love by Wally Runnels is a gritty tale that is enmeshed around the drug cartels in Mexico. Set in Mexicali, Mexico, our protagonist is Rocky, and just by the name alone, you know he is one tough customer. Rocky is a force to be reckoned with and as a creepy one armed assassin and a ex- marine, he is a gifted killer. Now he is on a mission to eliminate a newspaper editor who is getting a little too close to revealing some corruption and shady deals in the state police department. For a crime novel, this story is riveting, for action and suspense, this will keep you glued to your seat. There is plenty of action and a lot of twists and interesting turns to keep the pace hopping. Julietta Aguilar is the love interest in the story, and when she discovers something amazing during an archeological dig, strange things begin to transpire. A great mix of tension, a little romance and cold blooded killers, makes this story solid from beginning to the end. Highly recommend.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1643532664291633821">Archaeologist, Julietta Aguilar has just discovered a hidden chamber containing remains that appear to be those of a pair of intertwined lovers.   <span id="freeText1643532664291633821" style="display:none">Archaeologist, Julietta Aguilar has just discovered a hidden chamber containing remains that appear to be those of a pair of intertwined lovers. Rocky, an ex-Marine turned assassin, has just been hired by the police captain, Roberto Cruz, to murder a newspaper editor; Julietta’s father. What secrets was Cruz trying to keep from being unveiled? What happens when Rocky and Julietta’s worlds collide? <br /><br />Filled with twists and turns, ‘Twisted Love’ by Wally Runnels takes you on a wild ride through the grit and crime of a city immersed in corruption, drug cartels, and dirty cops. A bit slow in the beginning, once Runnels got my attention, I was hooked. This story is filled with intense action, cold blooded murder, the supernatural, and of course … romance. It will have you wondering who will make it out alive and if love will be enough. <br /><br />Warning, this novel is not for the faint at heart. It contains graphic violence, difficult sexual subject matter, rough language, and sex scenes. This read is deep and often times dark but the character and relationship development balance out the storyline. If you love crime novels, this one is for you! <br /><br />Disclosure: I received a complimentary copy of ‘Twisted Love’ for the purpose of review. Regardless, all opinions expressed are 100% my own. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText12547067821800814705" style="display:none">What struck me most about this cracking action novel, was the compelling and well developed characters. <div id="review_2196725635" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2196725635" />
    <a title="Book Blast" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72437516-book-blast"><img alt="Book Blast" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519305008p2/72437516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2196725635?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Book Blast" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Book Blast" href="/user/show/72437516-book-blast">Book Blast</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2196725635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3659206826734609386">If the thriller genre is your thing, pick up a copy of Twisted Love, and you will spend a truly exhilarating few hours embroiled in a fast-paced adventure that kept me on the edge of my seat until it's epic conclusion. Author Wally Runnels expertly intertwines the two plot lines of his protagonists, hired killer Rocky, and archaeologist Julietta. Throw in a crooked cop, dangerous Aztec spirits and unimaginable violence, and you have a novel that is bursting at the seams, and you will still want </span>
  <span id="freeText3659206826734609386" style="display:none">If the thriller genre is your thing, pick up a copy of Twisted Love, and you will spend a truly exhilarating few hours embroiled in a fast-paced adventure that kept me on the edge of my seat until it's epic conclusion. Author Wally Runnels expertly intertwines the two plot lines of his protagonists, hired killer Rocky, and archaeologist Julietta. Throw in a crooked cop, dangerous Aztec spirits and unimaginable violence, and you have a novel that is bursting at the seams, and you will still want more.<br /><br />Twisted Love is contemporary fiction at its finest, and I strongly suggest you add it to your book shelf. <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3659206826734609386" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2186891023" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7439506719868551973">Runnels is one of the first authors I’ve read in a while to make me really sit back and admire what I read. Cross-gene books are something we hear of a lot, or the claim at least, but seldom does an author really manage to pull it off in a way that you feel satisfied by what you’ve read for each of the genres mentioned. <br/><br/>There’s so much going on in Twisted Love. I’m a big fan of the 50’s era Hardboiled Pulp referenced in the book blurb, and I’m happy to say this lived up to the billing. Add in th</span>
  <span id="freeText7439506719868551973" style="display:none">Runnels is one of the first authors I’ve read in a while to make me really sit back and admire what I read. Cross-gene books are something we hear of a lot, or the claim at least, but seldom does an author really manage to pull it off in a way that you feel satisfied by what you’ve read for each of the genres mentioned. <br /><br />There’s so much going on in Twisted Love. I’m a big fan of the 50’s era Hardboiled Pulp referenced in the book blurb, and I’m happy to say this lived up to the billing. Add in the Love / Romance factor and this, for me, turned out to be a real winner.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1732576424" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1732576424" />
    <a title="Lynda Dickson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7863634-lynda-dickson"><img alt="Lynda Dickson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459810632p2/7863634.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1732576424?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lynda Dickson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lynda Dickson" href="/user/show/7863634-lynda-dickson">Lynda Dickson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/31750346-twisted-love">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Ages 18+</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7863634-lynda-dickson?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1732576424" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16018421679175246578">During an excavation in Mexico City, archaeologist Julietta Aguilar discovers a hidden chamber containing what appear to be the remains of a pair of intertwined lovers. When strange things start happening, she fears she may have released a malevolent spirit. Meanwhile, Roberto Cruz hires Rocky to assassinate Julietta's father, a journalist seeking to publish an exposé on Cruz himself. Both Julietta and Rocky struggle with demons from their past, but what will happen when their paths finally cros</span>
  <span id="freeText16018421679175246578" style="display:none">During an excavation in Mexico City, archaeologist Julietta Aguilar discovers a hidden chamber containing what appear to be the remains of a pair of intertwined lovers. When strange things start happening, she fears she may have released a malevolent spirit. Meanwhile, Roberto Cruz hires Rocky to assassinate Julietta's father, a journalist seeking to publish an exposé on Cruz himself. Both Julietta and Rocky struggle with demons from their past, but what will happen when their paths finally cross?<br /><br />The narrative alternates between Julietta's story, Rocky's story, and the story behind Julietta's archaeological discovery. The author sets a cracking pace that never lets up. Be warned, this book is full of graphic violence and several twisted relationships. A truly twisted love develops between two of the characters, but you just can't help but root for them. <br /><br />I wasn't a fan of the original cover [still featured here] and thought that Running Jaguar would feature more heavily than he does; I'm happy to see the author changed it. I'm interested to see if Rocky returns in another book or if he's walked off into the sunset. If so, I'll miss you, Rocky.<br /><br />Warnings: graphic violence, coarse language, sexual references, sex scenes.<br /><br />I received this book in return for an honest review.<br /><br />Full blog post (20 July): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://booksdirectonline.blogspot.com/2017/07/twisted-love-by-wally-runnels.html">https://booksdirectonline.blogspot.co...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16018421679175246578" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('abqRg3Rxx+3eLPAooxtAPmFEy+pU9HvMt11FKH8eu/V5t4usNpWhVWMSBNSx0zIT0GeCAykXf3oF0coGc8rCdw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Dv6srIXuH7cL0AsFLc2S34+HXeCmkbVWWW9KMJnOdY0e87aDxwp5D7bu//k/BeDyPqQUCdtyseDr48UelRoMDw==')})
  }

With a foreword by Dame Helen Mirren—the first foreword she has ever contributed.\n\nIn this striking compilation, Shakespeare historian Gerit Quealy and respected Japanese artist Sumié Hasegawa combine their knowledge and skill in this first and only book that examines every plant that appears in the works of Shakespeare.\n\nBotanical Shakespeare opens with a brief look at the Bard’s relationship to the plants mentioned in his works—a diversity that illuminates his knowledge of the science of botany, as well as the colloquy, revealing his unmatched skill for creating metaphorical connections and interweaving substantive philosophy. At the heart of the book are &quot;portraits&quot; of the over 170 flowers, fruits, grains, grasses, trees, herbs, seeds and vegetables that Shakespeare mentions in his plays and poems. Botanical Shakespeare features a gorgeous color illustration of each, giving a &quot;face&quot; to the name, alongside the specific text in which it appears and the character(s) who utter the lines in which it is mentioned.\n\nThis fascinating visual compendium also includes a dictionary describing each plant—such as Eglantine, a wild rose with a slight prickle, cherished for its singular scent, superior to any other rose; and the difference between apples and apple-john—along with indices listing the botanical by play/poem, by character, and genus for easy reference, ideal for gardeners and thoughtful birthday gift-giving.\n\nThis breathtaking, incomparable collection of exquisite artwork and companion quotes offers unique depth and insight into Shakespeare and his timeless work through the unusual perspective of the plants themselves.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"16282625506726576847\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n He argues this destruction will continue until Americans learn to heal the generational anguish of white supremacy, which is deeply embedded in all our bodies. Our collective agony doesn\'t just affect African Americans. White Americans suffer their own secondary trauma as well. So do blue Americans—our police.\n\nMy Grandmother\'s Hands is a call to action for all of us to recognize that racism is not about the head, but about the body, and introduces an alternative view of what we can do to grow beyond our entrenched racialized divide.\n\n\n\nPaves the way for a new, body-centered understanding of white supremacy—how it is literally in our blood and our nervous system.\n\n\nOffers a step-by-step solution—a healing process—in addition to incisive social commentary.\n\nResmaa Menakem, MSW, LICSW, is a therapist with decades of experience currently in private practice in Minneapolis, MN, specializing in trauma, body-centered psychotherapy, and violence prevention. He has appeared on the Oprah Winfrey Show and Dr. Phil as an expert on conflict and violence. Menakem has studied with bestselling authors Dr. David Schnarch (Passionate Marriage) and Dr. Bessel van der Kolk (The Body Keeps the Score).
